<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">теряти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terjati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wreck, ruin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, iterative of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">терети</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tereti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***теряться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:теряться.html>теря́ться</a> (5774)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терять.html>теря́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теряться.html>теря́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">terjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потеряться.html>потеря́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get lost, to disappear</li>
<li>to lose one's way</li>
<li>to lose one's presence of mind, to get flustered</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fail, to weaken <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">eyesight, hearing, memory, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терять.html>теря́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ря́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
<a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:потеряться.html>потеря́ться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:затеряться.html>затеря́ться</a> (знач. 1, 2); <a href = vnd.unilang:растеряться.html>растеря́ться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:потеряться.html>потеря́ться</a> (знач. 5).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-тер-</b>; суффикс: <b>-я</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***тесать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесать.html>теса́ть</a> (31950)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тесати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tesati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tesàti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tetḱ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесать.html>теса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tesátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to hew <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with an axe</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to make (something) by cutting with an axe</li>
<li>to shave the surface layer of <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with an axe</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — тесануть, отесать, обтесать.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tésnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теснить.html>тесни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tesnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потеснить.html>потесни́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стесни́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press, to crowd
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:теснить.html>тесни́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tesnítʹ</b> protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to press the enemy</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потеснить.html>потесни́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potesnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to squeeze, to be too tight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:теснить.html>тесни́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грудь.html>грудь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>tesnít</b> grudʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I feel/have a tightness in my chest</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стесни́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stesnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесниться.html>тесни́ться</a> (13357)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теснить.html>тесни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tesnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесниться.html>тесни́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tesnítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стесни́ться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потесниться.html>потесни́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crowd, to be herded, to cluster, to jostle one another</li>
<li>to be squeezed, to sit close</li>
<li><i>(thoughts, emotions etc)</i> to crowd</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теснить.html>тесни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tesnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tésnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tésno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***теснота.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:теснота.html>теснота́</a> (10980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>тесный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tesnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ота</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теснота.html>теснота́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tesnotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теснота.html>тесноты́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>narrowness; tightness; closeness</li>
<li>cram, crush
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  Андрей Юрьевич <a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>Курко́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrey_Kurkov" class="extiw" title="w:Andrey Kurkov">Andrey Yuryevich Kurkov</a>),  chapter 80, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>Зако́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улитка.html>ули́тки</a></cite>  | <cite>The Snail Law</cite> |  |  translated as George Bird, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Penguin_Lost" class="extiw" title="w:Penguin Lost">Penguin Lost</a></cite>, 2010:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:украшать.html>украша́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:елка.html>ёлку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вместе.html>вме́сте</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:поэтому.html>поэ́тому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> и́з-за <b><a href = vnd.unilang:теснота.html>тесноты́</a></b> ни́на <a href = vnd.unilang:умудриться.html>умудри́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рика</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ukrašáli jólku vse vméste. Poétomu býlo tésno, i íz-za <b>tesnotý</b> Nína umudrílasʹ razbítʹ dva šárika.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">They all decorated the New Year's tree together. So they were crowded, and because of the <b>crowding</b>, Nina managed to smash two balls.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:теснота.html>тесноте́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обида.html>оби́де</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>tesnoté</b>, da ne v obíde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the more the merrier</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ol><li>тесность</li>
<li>стеснённость</li></ol>

***тесный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>тесный</a> (3137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тѣснъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">těsnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*těsnъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">narrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. According to Václav Machek, it is related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στενός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stenós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">narrow, tight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thus making both derive from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ténh₂us</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tésnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тесне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тесне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tight, close, narrow</li>
<li>small
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сен</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mir <b>tésen</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it's a small world</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">short form only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> too tight, too narrow <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of clothing and shoes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:штаны.html>штаны́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сны</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne éti štaný <b>tésny</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">these trousers are too tight for me</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>те́с<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b> (<span title="написание в дореформенной орфографии" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">дореформ.</span> <span style="font-family: | Palatino Linotype | ">тѣсный</span>)
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a/c'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>тесне́е, тесне́й.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-тесн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***тесто.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесто.html>тесто</a> (9168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тѣсто</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">těsto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*těsto</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесто.html>те́сто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tésto</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесто.html>те́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесто.html>те́ста</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тесто.html>тест</a></b>)
</p>

***техасский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:техасский.html>теха́сский</a> (26688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">теха́с</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Texás</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***технический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:технический.html>техни́ческий</a> (1286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">те́хн(ика)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">téxn(ika)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:технический.html>техни́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">texníčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>technological</li>
<li>technical</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> engineering; mechanical</li>
<li>industrial</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тех</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чес<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3a✕~.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-техн-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ич-еск</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
